Reclaimed, twisted, and retold by the Octavia Project
Erik realizes this is a big opportunity for his kingdom-- he could rule both the land AND the sea! \n\nErik goes to sea-therapy and processes what it means to be a sea-citizen. After a few months, he has ceased hyperventilating when he breathes underwater. He adjusts. \n\nErik marries Ariel, but it is a political marriage. Ariel decides he will grow to love her over time... \n\nShe is still waiting... \n\n[img[alone mermaid]]\n\n[[Back|Witch]]
Ariel, the youngest daughter of the King of the sea, has become obsessed with the human world. She is known for her beautiful singing voice. \n\n[[Triton]]\n\n[img[mermaid swim]]\n\n\n
Ariel notices a cute marine biologist wandering around the science building at her University, a man called Tyler. They end up falling in love. Eventually, she trusts him enough to tell him of her secret previous life as a mermaid. \n\nTyler and Ariel spend long hours recounting details of her home, a fiercly deepening nostolgia that has been coloring Ariel's new life a little blue. \n\nThey buy a house boat and live half on the sea, half on land. \n\nAriel goes for long swims. \n\nThey are happy. \n\nThe end. \n\n[[Back|Witch]]\n

Ariel cannot stand to see her love suffering, his pain so similar to her old hurt. \n\nShe leaves her life under the sea and grants them both legs. They are relatively happy (and sometimes not.) \n\nYet she still longs for the sea. \n\nSometimes, at night, you can find Ariel tracing the shoreline with a bare foot, under the all-knowing moon. \n\n[[Back|previous()]]\n

Ursula-in-disguise enchants Erik and they are to be married. \n\n[[Evil]]
On the surface, however, she realizes with slow creeping certainity that she and her handsome Prince actually don't have much in common. \n\n[[University]]
Ursula betrays Ariel, and goes to the surface with Ariel's voice and a hot new bod. \n\n[[Marriage]]
Erik, terrified by Ariel's power over him, seeks out Ursula, the sea-witch, to ally against Ariel. \n\nShe tricks him and he is stuck in her garden, a shriveled sea-weed man forever. \n\nPOOR ERIK! \n\n[[Back|previous()]]
Ariel trades her voice for legs, to try to win the heart of Prince Erik. \n\n[[Voice]]
Ariel's father, Triton, becomes suspicious after Ariel misses a big singing concert. He has Ariel followed. Ariel, meanwhile, has followed a ship and fallen in love with a man she rescues from a storm. \n\n[[Fury]]
Erik adjusts quickly to his life under the sea. But sometimes, late at night, Ariel catches him watching the city lights up above...\n\n[[Sympathy]] \n\n[[Empathy]] \n\n[[Back|Witch]]
Ariel, shattered by her father's fury, goes to Ursula, the sea witch. \n\n[[Witch]]\n\n[img[sad mermaid]]\n
Ursula catches her in the act. She kills her.\n\n[[Back|previous()]]\n\n[img[mermaid rock]]\n
After a grueling year and a day of study, Ariel has learned enough to not depend on sneaky witches for favors. A newly intiated witch herself, she goes to the surface with her voice intact. \n\n[[Common]]
Ariel has become too entrenched in mer-politics to leave her life behind for Eric. She reverses the spell and gives him legs. \n\nHe lives on land, \n\nShe in the sea. \n\nFor a while, they write letters, sealed in a bottle, and meet for kisses off the side of his great ship. \n\nBut eventually, their meetings grow less and less frequent. \n\nThey grow apart. \n\nThe End. \n\n[[Back|previous()]]\n\n\n

Ariel, shocked by the Prince's anger, quickly reverses the spell. \n\nIt becomes a story he tells at dinner parties and court functions, "That time when that crazy mermaid dragged me to live at the bottom of the sea with her." His coterie grows weary of hearing it. \n\nThe prince marries eventually, (a young princess from a far away kingdom) but it is rumored that they live quite separate lives. He still goes out sailing, for months at a time. \n\nAriel never marries. \n\nThe end. \n\n[[Back|previous()]]\n
